## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

## Input Data

HTF range:  2026-02-28 05:00 → 2026-03-03 04:00
LTF range:  2026-03-03 01:00 → 2026-03-03 04:45
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

You are a professional cryptocurrency trader specializing in Smart Money Concepts (SMC).

## Input Data
Symbol:     BTC/USDT:USDT
HTF:        1h  (72 candles)
LTF:        15m  (16 candles)
HTF range:  2026-03-02 02:00 → 2026-03-05 01:00
LTF range:  2026-03-04 22:00 → 2026-03-05 01:45
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

You are a professional cryptocurrency trader specializing in Smart Money Concepts (SMC).

## Input Data
Symbol:     BTC/USDT:USDT
HTF:        1h  (72 candles)
LTF:        15m  (16 candles)
HTF range:  2026-03-03 08:00 → 2026-03-06 07:00
LTF range:  2026-03-06 03:30 → 2026-03-06 07:15
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

You are a professional cryptocurrency trader specializing in Smart Money Concepts (SMC).

## Input Data
Symbol:     BTC/USDT:USDT
HTF:        1h  (72 candles)
LTF:        15m  (16 candles)
HTF range:  2026-03-07 01:00 → 2026-03-10 00:00
LTF range:  2026-03-09 20:45 → 2026-03-10 00:30
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

You are a professional cryptocurrency trader specializing in Smart Money Concepts (SMC).

## Input Data
Symbol:     BTC/USDT:USDT
HTF:        1h  (72 candles)
LTF:        15m  (16 candles)
HTF range:  2026-03-10 04:00 → 2026-03-13 03:00
LTF range:  2026-03-13 00:00 → 2026-03-13 03:45
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

You are a professional cryptocurrency trader specializing in Smart Money Concepts (SMC).

## Input Data
Symbol:     BTC/USDT:USDT
HTF:        1h  (72 candles)
LTF:        15m  (16 candles)
HTF range:  2026-03-11 10:00 → 2026-03-14 09:00
LTF range:  2026-03-14 06:00 → 2026-03-14 09:45
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

You are a professional cryptocurrency trader specializing in Smart Money Concepts (SMC).

## Input Data
Symbol:     BTC/USDT:USDT
HTF:        1h  (72 candles)
LTF:        15m  (16 candles)
HTF range:  2026-03-14 00:00 → 2026-03-16 23:00
LTF range:  2026-03-16 19:45 → 2026-03-16 23:30
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

## Input Data

LTF:        15m  (16 candles)

LTF range:  2026-03-17 16:15 → 2026-03-17 20:00
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

You are a professional cryptocurrency trader specializing in Smart Money Concepts (SMC).

## Input Data
Symbol:     BTC/USDT:USDT
HTF:        1h  (72 candles)
LTF:        15m  (16 candles)
HTF range:  2026-03-15 02:00 → 2026-03-18 01:00
LTF range:  2026-03-17 21:45 → 2026-03-18 01:30
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

You are a professional cryptocurrency trader specializing in Smart Money Concepts (SMC).

## Input Data
Symbol:     BTC/USDT:USDT
HTF:        1h  (72 candles)
LTF:        15m  (16 candles)
HTF range:  2026-03-17 07:00 → 2026-03-20 06:00
LTF range:  2026-03-20 02:15 → 2026-03-20 06:00
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

You are a professional cryptocurrency trader specializing in Smart Money Concepts (SMC).

## Input Data
Symbol:     BTC/USDT:USDT
HTF:        1h  (72 candles)
LTF:        15m  (16 candles)

LTF range:  2026-03-24 14:15 → 2026-03-24 18:00
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

You are a professional cryptocurrency trader specializing in Smart Money Concepts (SMC).

## Input Data
Symbol:     BTC/USDT:USDT
HTF:        1h  (72 candles)
LTF:        15m  (16 candles)
HTF range:  2026-03-23 09:00 → 2026-03-26 08:00
LTF range:  2026-03-26 04:30 → 2026-03-26 08:15
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

## Input Data

LTF range:  2026-03-28 18:00 → 2026-03-28 21:45
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

LTF range:  2026-04-01 12:00 → 2026-04-01 15:45
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

## Input Data

LTF:        15m  (16 candles)
HTF range:  2026-04-01 20:00 → 2026-04-04 19:00
LTF range:  2026-04-04 15:15 → 2026-04-04 19:00
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

LTF range:  2026-04-06 05:15 → 2026-04-06 09:00
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

You are a professional cryptocurrency trader specializing in Smart Money Concepts (SMC).

## Input Data
Symbol:     BTC/USDT:USDT
HTF:        1h  (72 candles)
LTF:        15m  (16 candles)
HTF range:  2026-04-04 15:00 → 2026-04-07 14:00
LTF range:  2026-04-07 10:15 → 2026-04-07 14:00
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

You are a professional cryptocurrency trader specializing in Smart Money Concepts (SMC).

## Input Data
Symbol:     BTC/USDT:USDT
HTF:        1h  (72 candles)
LTF:        15m  (16 candles)
HTF range:  2026-04-06 02:00 → 2026-04-09 01:00
LTF range:  2026-04-08 22:00 → 2026-04-09 01:45
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

You are a professional cryptocurrency trader specializing in Smart Money Concepts (SMC).

## Input Data
Symbol:     BTC/USDT:USDT
HTF:        1h  (72 candles)
LTF:        15m  (16 candles)
HTF range:  2026-04-06 16:00 → 2026-04-09 15:00
LTF range:  2026-04-09 11:15 → 2026-04-09 15:00
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.

You are a professional cryptocurrency trader specializing in Smart Money Concepts (SMC).

## Input Data
Symbol:     BTC/USDT:USDT
HTF:        1h  (72 candles)
LTF:        15m  (16 candles)
HTF range:  2026-04-08 23:00 → 2026-04-11 22:00
LTF range:  2026-04-11 18:15 → 2026-04-11 22:00
FVG offset: 1.0 %

## Strategy
HTF FVG + LTF BOS (Fair Value Gap with Break of Structure confirmation)

Entry logic:
1. [HTF] Identify all valid Fair Value Gaps (FVGs).
   - Bullish FVG: candle[i+1].low > candle[i-1].high — an upward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes below the gap bottom.
   - Bearish FVG: candle[i+1].high < candle[i-1].low — a downward price gap.
     Invalidated when any subsequent candle closes above the gap top.

2. [LTF] Bullish setup:
   a. The lowest LTF swing low lies inside a valid bullish HTF FVG, or just
      below it within the configured offset (% of FVG range).
   b. A prior LTF swing high (the last one before the swing low) acts as the
      Break of Structure (BOS) level.
   c. Price closes above that BOS level after the swing low — confirming the
      bullish directional shift.

3. [LTF] Bearish setup:
   a. The highest LTF swing high lies inside a valid bearish HTF FVG, or just
      above it within the configured offset.
   b. A prior LTF swing low (the last one before the swing high) acts as the
      BOS level.
   c. Price closes below that BOS level after the swing high — confirming the
      bearish directional shift.

4. [LTF] Stop Loss:
    - For bullish entries: just below the swing low (which is inside the FVG).
    - For bearish entries: just above the swing high (which is inside the FVG).

5. [HTF] Take Profit:
    - For bullish entries: swing highs or low of bearish FVG.
    - For bearish entries: swing lows or high of bullish FVG.

6. [LTF] Entry Order:
    For both bullish and bearish setups, limit order which gives risk-reward at least 2:1 based on the defined stop loss and take profit levels.

The HTF FVG is the Point of Interest (POI) / demand or supply zone.
The LTF swing point marks the liquidity sweep / wick into that zone.
The BOS confirms that smart money has absorbed liquidity and is pushing price.
